   -framework Cocoa -framework IOSurface

cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/../shared/resources/pdf.html build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/pdf.html
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/../shared/resources/pdf.pdf build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/pdf.pdf
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/../shared/resources/window_icon.1x.png build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/window_icon.1x.png
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/../shared/resources/window_icon.2x.png build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/window_icon.2x.png
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/expired_cert.pem build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/expired_cert.pem
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/localhost_cert.pem build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/localhost_cert.pem
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/ok_cert.pem build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/ok_cert.pem
cd build/tests/ceftests && cmake-E copy tests/ceftests/resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/root_ca_cert.pem build/tests/ceftests/Release/ceftests.app/Contents/Resources/net/data/ssl/certificates/root_ca_cert.pem
cmake-E cmake_progress_start build/CMakeFiles 0
